window.successDataCheck = function (data) {
  try {
    if(data.data) {
      var dataString = Object.prototype.toString.call(data.data);
      if(dataString === '[object Object]' || dataString === '[object Array]') {
        return data.data
      }
    }
  } catch (error) { }
  return { "enable": false, "isDefault": true };
}
window.asyncSuccessDataCheck = function (data) {
  try { 
      if(data.data) {
      var dataString = Object.prototype.toString.call(data.data);
      if(dataString === '[object Object]' || dataString === '[object Array]') {
        return data.data
      }
    }
  } catch (error) {}
  return { data: { "enable": false, "isDefault": true } }
}

window.handleOfferTagData = function (data) {
  try {
    if (data && data.offerList && data.offerList.length > 0) {
      for (var i = 0; i < data.offerList.length; i++) {
        var offerData = data.offerList[i] || {};
        var offerTagData = offerData.marketOfferTag || {};
        for (var j in window.data.tagConfig) {
          var currentTagData = window.data.tagConfig[j];
          var insertData = tagFindForAry(currentTagData, offerTagData[j]);
          if (!offerData.feMapping) {
            offerData.feMapping = {};
          }
          offerData.feMapping[j] = insertData;
        }
      }
    }
  } catch (error) { console.log('tag方象鯉塀呟械'); }
  function tagFindForAry(data, ary) {
    if (!ary || !data) {
      return {};
    }
    var result = {};
    for (var i in data) {
      if (ary.indexOf(data[i]) !== -1) {
        result[i] = true;
      } else {
        result[i] = false;
      }
    }
    return result;
  }
}
